import pandas as pd
from caas_jupyter_tools import display_dataframe_to_user

# Reload sources
src_path = "/mnt/data/Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_Categorised_v13_With_TDD_Risk.xlsx"
xls = pd.ExcelFile(src_path)
prod = pd.read_excel(xls, "Production")
eng = pd.read_excel(xls, "Engineering")

# Helper to convert Excel col label to zero-based index
def xl_col_to_idx(col_label):
    col_label = col_label.upper()
    idx = 0
    for ch in col_label:
        idx = idx * 26 + (ord(ch) - ord('A') + 1)
    return idx - 1

out_path = "/mnt/data/Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_Top10_Phase_v19.xlsx"
with pd.ExcelWriter(out_path, engine="xlsxwriter") as writer:
    prod.to_excel(writer, index=False, sheet_name="Production")
    eng.to_excel(writer, index=False, sheet_name="Engineering")
    # Minimal formatting
    for sheet_name, df in [("Production", prod), ("Engineering", eng)]:
        ws = writer.sheets[sheet_name]
        ws.set_column(0, 0, 30)
        ws.set_column(1, 1, 12)
        ws.set_column(2, 2, 78)
        ws.set_column(3, 3, 92)
        cols = df.columns.tolist()
        if "Why — technical" in cols:
            i = cols.index("Why — technical")

        if "Impact (1-10)" in cols: ws.set_column(cols.index("Impact (1-10)"), cols.index("Impact (1-10)"), 14)

as a team of expert game designers (general, level , technical, art, combat etc) critic this and assess what is missing

[ASSISTANT]
Here’s a straight critique from a cross-discipline design team, then a list of concrete missing risks. I’m only calling out problems, not fixes.

# Verdict
Good first pass, but it skews high level and systems-centric. Several core areas that routinely blow up schedule and quality are either lightly touched or absent. Some items overlap, which will blur ownership and weaken accountability.

# Overlap or ambiguity in the current list
- Partner hooks vs side modes cannibalising the core loop reads twice with different labels. Pick one lens, or you will double-count the same failure.
- Content lock and scope breadth vs depth both target the MVP slice. Distinguish content change control from slice definition or teams will ignore one.
- Combat readability and camera readability both touch feedback. Separate what is camera framing vs on-screen signalling.

# Material gaps to add
## Governance, definition and contracts
- Design change control is absent for Live. Risk: design work lands out of band after content lock, creating “last minute” builds that destabilise release.
- Design–Art contract is missing. Risk: art direction and kit-of-parts do not support intended mechanics, producing pretty but unreadable spaces.
- Design–Audio contract is missing. Risk: combat and state feedback do not have an agreed audio grammar, reducing clarity and impact.
- Design–Data contract is under-specified. Risk: features ship without agreed events, properties, and IDs, making tuning blind.

## Monetisation and ratings
- Monetisation design guardrails are missing. Risk: loops over-reward or time-gate in ways that read as pay pressure and harm retention.
- Ratings and regional compliance are absent. Risk: PEGI/ESRB and regional rules clash with intended content, forcing late cuts or resubmissions.

## Tools and authoring pipelines
- Designer authoring tool maturity is not covered. Risk: level and quest authors block on engineering, causing hidden queue time and spec drift.
- Content taxonomy and ID hygiene are missing. Risk: duplicate or colliding IDs across quests, items, achievements, cosmetics, and events.

## Progression, economy, and pacing depth
- Session length and fatigue targets are not stated. Risk: MVP pacing either exhausts players or never reaches a dopamine peak.
- Economy sinks across side modes are not defined. Risk: off-core activities inflate currency and break progression.
- Difficulty curve cohesion across handcrafted and partner content is not addressed. Risk: players hit sudden spikes or troughs when switching sources.

## Onboarding and retention
- Tutorial resilience to updates is omitted. Risk: patches invalidate the golden path, creating untracked drop-offs.
- Early retention targets tied to design hypotheses are missing. Risk: design cannot judge success or failure of the first 30 minutes.

## Social, safety, and grief vectors
- Physics and collision griefing are not called out. Risk: knockback, body blocking, or ragdoll loops create harassment vectors.
- AFK and bot farming patterns are missing. Risk: progression and economy are distorted by unattended play.

## Cross-platform playability
- Controller vs keyboard layout density is only partially covered. Risk: crucial actions bury on one input set, creating an unfair meta.
- Platform TRC/TCR design implications are absent. Risk: UI flows and terminology fail first-party checks and delay release.

## Combat and encounter design depth
- Skill floor vs skill ceiling alignment is not stated. Risk: either new players churn or veterans see no mastery path.
- Boss and set-piece staging rules are missing. Risk: multi-phase fights collapse into unreadable damage races.

## Level design and world clarity
- Streaming and occlusion design constraints are not referenced. Risk: pop-in or culling breaks navigation and combat readability.
- Landmark and breadcrumb budgets lack quantitative targets. Risk: later map additions drift from the readability standard.

## UGC and creator-facing concerns
- Streamability and spectate readability are not considered. Risk: content is hard to watch, reducing organic discovery.
- UGC content guidelines at a design level are thin. Risk: quality and tone vary so widely that the world loses coherence.

## Accessibility and localisation
- Localisation and culturalisation risks are missing. Risk: text expansion breaks UI, motifs or gestures miss in some regions.
- Accessibility coverage is listed, but there is no acceptance gate per feature. Risk: features ship without required toggles or comfort options.

## Analytics and experimentation
- Experiment design is not covered. Risk: A/B tests confound multiple variables, creating false positives and bad calls.
- KPI ladders per feature are missing. Risk: teams cannot tie design changes to D1, D7, D30 impacts and stall tuning.

## Partner content specifics
- Tone and canon alignment rules for partner IP are missing. Risk: world coherence breaks and the core loop message blurs.
- Approval and content freeze windows for partners are not in design space. Risk: late partner edits force emergency rebuilds.

# Items to tighten in the existing entries
- “Corruption cleaning unclear” is good, but it should explicitly include player agency tests, reward timing, and telegraph tiers. Right now it reads generic.
- “Player Space overruns MVP” should call out storage burden and menu friction, not just scope size. Those two are the usual kill shots.
- “Cosmetic rarity and theme inconsistency” needs an explicit drop table relationship. Without that, art can be consistent while the economy still feels wrong.
- “No design telemetry for validation” should require exact event names and properties in the spec. As written, it is easy to claim “we have some events”.

design_df = pd.DataFrame(design_rows)
# Compute Risk Score
design_df["Risk Score (LxI)"] = design_df["Likelihood (1-10)"] * design_df["Impact (1-10)"]

# Deduplicate by Category + Risk + Phase
design_df = design_df.drop_duplicates(subset=["Category","Phase","Risk"]).reset_index(drop=True)

# Write a new workbook v20 with the Design tab added and Top 10 updated to include Design
out_path = "/mnt/data/Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_with_Design_v20.xlsx"
with pd.ExcelWriter(out_path, engine="xlsxwriter") as writer:
    prod_df.to_excel(writer, index=False, sheet_name="Production")
    eng_df.to_excel(writer, index=False, sheet_name="Engineering")
    design_df.to_excel(writer, index=False, sheet_name="Design")

    # Format the three sheets (hide Why — technical on screen but keep it present)
    for name, df in [("Production", prod_df), ("Engineering", eng_df), ("Design", design_df)]:
        ws = writer.sheets[name]
        ws.set_column(0, 0, 30)   # Category
        ws.set_column(1, 1, 12)   # Phase
        ws.set_column(2, 2, 64)   # Risk
        ws.set_column(3, 3, 86)   # Why it would occur
        # Hide technical column if present
        cols = df.columns.tolist()
        if "Why — technical" in cols:
            idx = cols.index("Why — technical")
            ws.set_column(idx, idx, 80, None, {'hidden': True})
        else:
            # For the Design sheet we used 'Why — technical' as key; ensure it's present
            pass
        # Numbers
        if "Likelihood (1-10)" in cols: ws.set_column(cols.index("Likelihood (1-10)"), cols.index("Likelihood (1-10)"), 14)
        if "Impact (1-10)" in cols: ws.set_column(cols.index("Impact (1-10)"), cols.index("Impact (1-10)"), 14)
        if "Risk Score (LxI)" in cols: ws.set_column(cols.index("Risk Score (LxI)"), cols.index("Risk Score (LxI)"), 18)
        if "Owner" in cols: ws.set_column(cols.index("Owner"), cols.index("Owner"), 20)
        ws.freeze_panes(1, 0)
        ws.autofilter(0, 0, len(df), len(df.columns)-1)

    # Build Top 10 by Phase with helper columns on this sheet only (hidden)
    ws_t = writer.book.add_worksheet("Top 10 by Phase")
    max_rows = 4000
    helpers = [
        ("Prod_MVP",       "Production",  "MVP",        "BA"),
        ("Prod_PreAlpha",  "Production",  "Pre-Alpha",  "BB"),
        ("Prod_Live",      "Production",  "Live",       "BC"),
        ("Eng_MVP",        "Engineering", "MVP",        "BD"),
        ("Eng_PreAlpha",   "Engineering", "Pre-Alpha",  "BE"),
        ("Eng_Live",       "Engineering", "Live",       "BF"),
        ("Des_MVP",        "Design",      "MVP",        "BG"),
        ("Des_PreAlpha",   "Design",      "Pre-Alpha",  "BH"),
        ("Des_Live",       "Design",      "Live",       "BI"),
    ]
    # Write helper formulas
    for name, area, phase, col in helpers:
        ws_t.write(0, 0, "")  # keep top-left clean
        col_idx = sum([(ord(c)-64)*26**i for i,c in enumerate(col[::-1])]) - 1
        ws_t.write(0, col_idx, f"{name} keys (hidden)")
        for r in range(2, max_rows+1):
            formula = f'=IF(TRIM({area}!$B{r})="{phase}", {area}!$H{r}+ROW()/{100000}, "")'
            ws_t.write_formula(r-1, col_idx, formula)
        ws_t.set_column(col_idx, col_idx, 2, None, {'hidden': True})

    # Place nine Top-10 blocks
    blocks = [
        ("MVP", "Production", 0, 0, "BA"),
        ("MVP", "Engineering", 0, 12, "BD"),
        ("MVP", "Design", 0, 24, "BG"),
        ("Pre-Alpha", "Production", 24, 0, "BB"),
        ("Pre-Alpha", "Engineering", 24, 12, "BE"),
        ("Pre-Alpha", "Design", 24, 24, "BH"),
        ("Live", "Production", 48, 0, "BC"),
        ("Live", "Engineering", 48, 12, "BF"),
        ("Live", "Design", 48, 24, "BI"),
    ]
    headers = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why — technical","Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner"]
    for phase, area, top, left, key_col in blocks:
        ws_t.write(top, left, f"{phase} — Top 10 ({area})")
        for i, h in enumerate(headers):
            ws_t.write(top+1, left+i, h)

        # Ranges from source sheets
        sheet = area
        key_rng   = f"${key_col}$2:${key_col}${max_rows}"
        cat_rng   = f"{sheet}!$A$2:$A${max_rows}"
        phase_rng = f"{sheet}!$B$2:$B${max_rows}"
        risk_rng  = f"{sheet}!$C$2:$C${max_rows}"
        why_rng   = f"{sheet}!$D$2:$D${max_rows}"
        whyt_rng  = f"{sheet}!$E$2:$E${max_rows}"
        like_rng  = f"{sheet}!$F$2:$F${max_rows}"
        imp_rng   = f"{sheet}!$G$2:$G${max_rows}"
        score_rng = f"{sheet}!$H$2:$H${max_rows}"
        owner_rng = f"{sheet}!$I$2:$I${max_rows}"

        row_of_k = f"MATCH(LARGE({key_rng}, ROW($A1)), {key_rng}, 0)"
        ws_t.write_formula(top+2, left+0, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({cat_rng}, {row_of_k}), \"\")")
        ws_t.write_formula(top+2, left+1, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({phase_rng}, {row_of_k}), \"\")")
        ws_t.write_formula(top+2, left+2, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({risk_rng}, {row_of_k}), \"\")")
        ws_t.write_formula(top+2, left+3, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({why_rng}, {row_of_k}), \"\")")
        ws_t.write_formula(top+2, left+4, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({whyt_rng}, {row_of_k}), \"\")")
        ws_t.write_formula(top+2, left+5, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({like_rng}, {row_of_k}), \"\")")
        ws_t.write_formula(top+2, left+6, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({imp_rng}, {row_of_k}), \"\")")
        ws_t.write_formula(top+2, left+7, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({score_rng}, {row_of_k}), \"\")")
        ws_t.write_formula(top+2, left+8, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({owner_rng}, {row_of_k}), \"\")")

        for r in range(1, 10):
            row_k = f"MATCH(LARGE({key_rng}, ROW($A1)+{r}), {key_rng}, 0)"
            ws_t.write_formula(top+2+r, left+0, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({cat_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")
            ws_t.write_formula(top+2+r, left+1, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({phase_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")
            ws_t.write_formula(top+2+r, left+2, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({risk_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")
            ws_t.write_formula(top+2+r, left+3, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({why_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")
            ws_t.write_formula(top+2+r, left+4, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({whyt_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")
            ws_t.write_formula(top+2+r, left+5, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({like_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")
            ws_t.write_formula(top+2+r, left+6, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({imp_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")
            ws_t.write_formula(top+2+r, left+7, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({score_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")
            ws_t.write_formula(top+2+r, left+8, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({owner_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")

        # Widths
        ws_t.set_column(left+0, left+0, 28)
        ws_t.set_column(left+1, left+1, 10)
        ws_t.set_column(left+2, left+2, 60)
        ws_t.set_column(left+3, left+3, 90)
        ws_t.set_column(left+4, left+4, 80, None, {'hidden': True})
        ws_t.set_column(left+5, left+7, 14)
        ws_t.set_column(left+8, left+8, 20)

# Surface link
display_dataframe_to_user("Download workbook with Design tab wired into Top-10", pd.DataFrame({"File":[out_path]}))

# Build consolidated Design risks DataFrame (as above)
design_rows = []

def add_row(cat, phase, risk, why, whytech, like, imp, owner):
    design_rows.append({
        "Category":cat, "Phase":phase, "Risk":risk,
        "Why it would occur":why, "Why — technical":whytech,
        "Likelihood (1-10)":like, "Impact (1-10)":imp, "Owner":owner
    })

add_row("Design Leadership & Governance","MVP","Design leadership bandwidth is over-stretched",
        "Many juniors need review while few senior designers can approve.",
        "High review and mentoring load on a small set of leads creates long queues; briefs and gates stall.",
        8,8,"Game Director")
add_row("Level Design","MVP","No Level Design Lead for multiple junior LDs",
        "Several junior LDs lack a dedicated lead; quality varies and iteration slows.",
        "No owner for metrics, readability rules and blockout standards; more late rework.",
        8,8,"Game Director")
add_row("Core Systems & Progression","MVP","No dedicated Economy or Systems Designer",
        "Progression and rewards go unowned; grind or inflation results.",
        "No owner for tables, curves and sinks; pacing changes land late and untested.",
        8,9,"Head of Product")
add_row("Animation Leadership","MVP","Lead Animator role is vacant",
        "Animation timing and combat feel lack senior ownership.",
        "Hit-reacts, cancels and locomotion polish fall behind; combat feels floaty or stiff.",
        8,9,"Game Director")
add_row("QA for Design","MVP","QA headcount too low for design validation",
        "Single QA cannot cover playtests, telemetry checks and regression.",
        "Design bugs and tuning gaps land in public builds; learning loops slow.",
        8,8,"QA")

# Governance/contracts/monetisation/compliance
add_row("Governance","Live","Design change control absent for Live",
        "Late design changes after content locks destabilise builds.",
        "No change-control flow for Live; emergency edits bypass review and regression.",
        7,8,"Design Director")
add_row("Design–Art Contract","MVP","Art kits do not support intended mechanics",
        "Assets are pretty but do not communicate state or affordances.",
        "No contract linking kit-of-parts to mechanic readability; missing designer-facing DO/DON'T rules.",
        7,8,"Art Director")
add_row("Design–Data Contract","MVP","Feature ships without agreed events and IDs",
        "Teams assume analytics will be added later; nothing lines up.",
        "Event names, properties and IDs not signed off; funnels break; dashboards unusable.",
        8,8,"Data Designer")
add_row("Monetisation","Live","Monetisation guardrails missing",
        "Loops over-reward or time-gate in ways that feel predatory.",
        "No policy for rate limits, earn-to-spend balance and price ladders; tests misread.",
        6,9,"Economy Designer")

# Compute score
design_df = pd.DataFrame(design_rows)
design_df["Risk Score (LxI)"] = design_df["Likelihood (1-10)"] * design_df["Impact (1-10)"]

# Write workbook with Design tab and Top 10 sheet wired (Production/Engineering unchanged)
out_path = "/mnt/data/Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_with_Design_v20.xlsx"
with pd.ExcelWriter(out_path, engine="xlsxwriter") as writer:
    prod_df.to_excel(writer, index=False, sheet_name="Production")
    eng_df.to_excel(writer, index=False, sheet_name="Engineering")
    design_df.to_excel(writer, index=False, sheet_name="Design")

    # Format sheets
    for name, df in [("Production", prod_df), ("Engineering", eng_df), ("Design", design_df)]:
        ws = writer.sheets[name]
        ws.set_column(0, 0, 30)
        ws.set_column(1, 1, 12)
        ws.set_column(2, 2, 64)
        ws.set_column(3, 3, 86)
        cols = df.columns.tolist()
        if "Why — technical" in cols:
            idx = cols.index("Why — technical")
            ws.set_column(idx, idx, 80, None, {'hidden': True})
        if "Likelihood (1-10)" in cols: ws.set_column(cols.index("Likelihood (1-10)"), cols.index("Likelihood (1-10)"), 14)
        if "Impact (1-10)" in cols: ws.set_column(cols.index("Impact (1-10)"), cols.index("Impact (1-10)"), 14)
        if "Risk Score (LxI)" in cols: ws.set_column(cols.index("Risk Score (LxI)"), cols.index("Risk Score (LxI)"), 18)
        if "Owner" in cols: ws.set_column(cols.index("Owner"), cols.index("Owner"), 20)
        ws.freeze_panes(1, 0)
        ws.autofilter(0, 0, len(df), len(df.columns)-1)

    # Top 10 by Phase sheet with helpers (hidden)
    ws_t = writer.book.add_worksheet("Top 10 by Phase")
    max_rows = 4000
    helpers = [
        ("Prod_MVP",       "Production",  "MVP",        "BA"),
        ("Prod_PreAlpha",  "Production",  "Pre-Alpha",  "BB"),
        ("Prod_Live",      "Production",  "Live",       "BC"),
        ("Eng_MVP",        "Engineering", "MVP",        "BD"),
        ("Eng_PreAlpha",   "Engineering", "Pre-Alpha",  "BE"),
        ("Eng_Live",       "Engineering", "Live",       "BF"),
        ("Des_MVP",        "Design",      "MVP",        "BG"),
        ("Des_PreAlpha",   "Design",      "Pre-Alpha",  "BH"),
        ("Des_Live",       "Design",      "Live",       "BI"),
    ]
    # Helper formulas
    def col_to_idx(col):
        col = col.upper()
        n=0
        for ch in col:
            n = n*26 + (ord(ch)-64)
        return n-1
    for name, area, phase, col in helpers:
        ci = col_to_idx(col)
        ws_t.write(0, ci, f"{name} keys (hidden)")
        for r in range(2, max_rows+1):
            ws_t.write_formula(r-1, ci, f'=IF(TRIM({area}!$B{r})="{phase}", {area}!$H{r}+ROW()/{100000}, "")')
        ws_t.set_column(ci, ci, 2, None, {'hidden': True})

    # Blocks
    blocks = [
        ("MVP", "Production", 0, 0, "BA"),
        ("MVP", "Engineering", 0, 12, "BD"),
        ("MVP", "Design", 0, 24, "BG"),
        ("Pre-Alpha", "Production", 24, 0, "BB"),
        ("Pre-Alpha", "Engineering", 24, 12, "BE"),
        ("Pre-Alpha", "Design", 24, 24, "BH"),
        ("Live", "Production", 48, 0, "BC"),
        ("Live", "Engineering", 48, 12, "BF"),
        ("Live", "Design", 48, 24, "BI"),
    ]
    headers = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why — technical","Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner"]
    for phase, area, top, left, key_col in blocks:
        ws_t.write(top, left, f"{phase} — Top 10 ({area})")
        for i, h in enumerate(headers):
            ws_t.write(top+1, left+i, h)

        key_rng   = f"${key_col}$2:${key_col}${max_rows}"
        cat_rng   = f"{area}!$A$2:$A${max_rows}"
        phase_rng = f"{area}!$B$2:$B${max_rows}"
        risk_rng  = f"{area}!$C$2:$C${max_rows}"
        why_rng   = f"{area}!$D$2:$D${max_rows}"
        whyt_rng  = f"{area}!$E$2:$E${max_rows}"
        like_rng  = f"{area}!$F$2:$F${max_rows}"
        imp_rng   = f"{area}!$G$2:$G${max_rows}"
        score_rng = f"{area}!$H$2:$H${max_rows}"
        owner_rng = f"{area}!$I$2:$I${max_rows}"

        row_of_k = f"MATCH(LARGE({key_rng}, ROW($A1)), {key_rng}, 0)"
        for r_offset in range(0,10):
            row_k = row_of_k if r_offset==0 else f"MATCH(LARGE({key_rng}, ROW($A1)+{r_offset}), {key_rng}, 0)"
            base_row = top+2+r_offset
            ws_t.write_formula(base_row, left+0, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({cat_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")
            ws_t.write_formula(base_row, left+1, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({phase_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")
            ws_t.write_formula(base_row, left+2, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({risk_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")
            ws_t.write_formula(base_row, left+3, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({why_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")
            ws_t.write_formula(base_row, left+4, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({whyt_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")
            ws_t.write_formula(base_row, left+5, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({like_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")
            ws_t.write_formula(base_row, left+6, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({imp_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")
            ws_t.write_formula(base_row, left+7, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({score_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")
            ws_t.write_formula(base_row, left+8, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({owner_rng}, {row_k}), \"\")")

        # Widths
        ws_t.set_column(left+0, left+0, 28)
        ws_t.set_column(left+1, left+1, 10)
        ws_t.set_column(left+2, left+2, 60)
        ws_t.set_column(left+3, left+3, 90)
        ws_t.set_column(left+4, left+4, 80, None, {'hidden': True})
        ws_t.set_column(left+5, left+7, 14)
        ws_t.set_column(left+8, left+8, 20)

# Show a link to the file
display_dataframe_to_user("Workbook with Design tab wired into Top-10 (v20)", pd.DataFrame({"Download":[out_path]}))

files = sorted(glob.glob("/mnt/data/*.xlsx"))
pd.DataFrame({"files": files})

design_df = pd.DataFrame(rows, columns=["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why — technical","Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Owner"])
design_df["Risk Score (LxI)"] = design_df["Likelihood (1-10)"] * design_df["Impact (1-10)"]

out_path = "/mnt/data/Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_Design_v20.xlsx"
with pd.ExcelWriter(out_path, engine="xlsxwriter") as writer:
    design_df.to_excel(writer, index=False, sheet_name="Design")
    ws = writer.sheets["Design"]
    ws.set_column(0, 0, 30)
    ws.set_column(1, 1, 12)
    ws.set_column(2, 2, 64)
    ws.set_column(3, 3, 86)
    ws.set_column(4, 4, 80, None, {'hidden': True})
    ws.set_column(5, 7, 14)
    ws.set_column(8, 8, 20)
    ws.freeze_panes(1, 0)
    ws.autofilter(0, 0, len(design_df), len(design_df.columns)-1)
    # Top 10 by Phase for Design only
    t = writer.book.add_worksheet("Top 10 by Phase")
    max_rows = 4000
    # helper columns BG/BH/BI
    def col_to_idx(col):
        col = col.upper()
        n=0
        for ch in col:
            n = n*26 + (ord(ch)-64)
        return n-1
    for phase, col in [("MVP","BG"),("Pre-Alpha","BH"),("Live","BI")]:
        ci = col_to_idx(col)
        t.write(0, ci, f"Design_{phase}_keys")
        for r in range(2, max_rows+1):
            t.write_formula(r-1, ci, f'=IF(TRIM(Design!$B{r})="{phase}", Design!$H{r}+ROW()/{100000}, "")')
        t.set_column(ci, ci, 2, None, {'hidden': True})
    # Blocks
    headers = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why — technical","Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner"]
    blocks = [("MVP",0,0,"BG"),("Pre-Alpha",24,0,"BH"),("Live",48,0,"BI")]
    for phase, top, left, key_col in blocks:
        t.write(top, left, f"{phase} — Top 10 (Design)")
        for i, h in enumerate(headers): t.write(top+1, left+i, h)
        key_rng   = f"${key_col}$2:${key_col}${max_rows}"
        cat_rng   = f"Design!$A$2:$A${max_rows}"
        phase_rng = f"Design!$B$2:$B${max_rows}"
        risk_rng  = f"Design!$C$2:$C${max_rows}"
        why_rng   = f"Design!$D$2:$D${max_rows}"
        whyt_rng  = f"Design!$E$2:$E${max_rows}"
        like_rng  = f"Design!$F$2:$F${max_rows}"
        imp_rng   = f"Design!$G$2:$G${max_rows}"
        score_rng = f"Design!$H$2:$H${max_rows}"
        owner_rng = f"Design!$I$2:$I${max_rows}"
        row_of_k  = f"MATCH(LARGE({key_rng}, ROW($A1)), {key_rng}, 0)"
        for r_off in range(0,10):
            rk = row_of_k if r_off==0 else f"MATCH(LARGE({key_rng}, ROW($A1)+{r_off}), {key_rng}, 0)"
            base = top+2+r_off
            t.write_formula(base, left+0, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({cat_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+1, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({phase_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+2, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({risk_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+3, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({why_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+4, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({whyt_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+5, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({like_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+6, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({imp_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+7, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({score_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+8, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({owner_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
        # widths
        t.set_column(left+0, left+0, 28)
        t.set_column(left+1, left+1, 10)
        t.set_column(left+2, left+2, 60)
        t.set_column(left+3, left+3, 90)
        t.set_column(left+4, left+4, 80, None, {'hidden': True})
        t.set_column(left+5, left+7, 14)
        t.set_column(left+8, left+8, 20)

display_dataframe_to_user("Download Design risk register with wired Top-10 (v20)", pd.DataFrame({"Download":["/mnt/data/Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_Design_v20.xlsx"]}))

import os, glob, pandas as pd
from caas_jupyter_tools import display_dataframe_to_user

base_path = "/mnt/data/Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_Categorised_v13_With_TDD_Risk.xlsx"

# Verify the base workbook with Production & Engineering exists
if not os.path.exists(base_path):
    # If it's not present, try to find a recent file that likely contains those tabs
    candidates = sorted(glob.glob("/mnt/data/*.xlsx"), reverse=True)
    raise FileNotFoundError(f"Base workbook not found at {base_path}. Files available: {candidates[:10]}")

# Load Production and Engineering
xls = pd.ExcelFile(base_path)
expected_tabs = xls.sheet_names

def safe_read(sheet_name):
    if sheet_name not in expected_tabs:
        raise ValueError(f"Required sheet '{sheet_name}' not found in {base_path}. Found sheets: {expected_tabs}")
    return pd.read_excel(xls, sheet_name)

prod_df = safe_read("Production")
eng_df  = safe_read("Engineering")

# Normalise columns to the canonical set used by Top-10 formulas
canonical_cols = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why — technical",
                  "Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner"]

def normalise(df):
    # Add missing columns
    for c in canonical_cols:
        if c not in df.columns:
            df[c] = "" if c not in ["Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)"] else pd.NA
    # Compute Risk Score if possible
    if "Risk Score (LxI)" in df.columns:
        try:
            like = pd.to_numeric(df["Likelihood (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
            imp  = pd.to_numeric(df["Impact (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
            rs   = like * imp
            # Only overwrite where both are valid numbers
            df.loc[like.notna() & imp.notna(), "Risk Score (LxI)"] = rs
        except Exception:
            pass
    # Reorder
    df = df[canonical_cols]
    # Trim Phase values to reduce matching issues
    df["Phase"] = df["Phase"].astype(str).str.strip()
    return df

prod_df = normalise(prod_df)
eng_df  = normalise(eng_df)

# Build consolidated Design DF (same canonical structure)

 "Hit-reacts, cancels and locomotion polish fall behind; combat feels floaty or stiff.",
 8,9,"Game Director"),
("QA for Design","MVP","QA headcount too low for design validation",
 "Single QA cannot cover playtests, telemetry checks and regression.",
 "Design bugs and tuning gaps land in public builds; learning loops slow.",
 8,8,"QA"),
("Governance","Live","Design change control absent for Live",
 "Late design changes after content locks destabilise builds.",
 "No change-control flow for Live; emergency edits bypass review and regression.",
 7,8,"Design Director"),
("Design–Art Contract","MVP","Art kits do not support intended mechanics",
 "Assets are pretty but do not communicate state or affordances.",
 "No contract linking kit-of-parts to mechanic readability; missing designer-facing DO/DON'T rules.",
 7,8,"Art Director"),
("Design–Data Contract","MVP","Feature ships without agreed events and IDs",
 "Teams assume analytics will be added later; nothing lines up.",
 "Event names, properties and IDs not signed off; funnels break; dashboards unusable.",
 8,8,"Data Designer"),
("Monetisation","Live","Monetisation guardrails missing",
 "Loops over-reward or time-gate in ways that feel predatory.",
 "No policy for rate limits, earn-to-spend balance and price ladders; tests misread.",
 6,9,"Economy Designer"),
]

design_df = pd.DataFrame(rows, columns=["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why — technical","Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Owner"])
design_df["Risk Score (LxI)"] = pd.to_numeric(design_df["Likelihood (1-10)"]) * pd.to_numeric(design_df["Impact (1-10)"])
design_df = design_df[canonical_cols]

# Write full workbook with 3 tabs and 9 Top-10 blocks
out_path = "/mnt/data/Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_ALL_v21.xlsx"
with pd.ExcelWriter(out_path, engine="xlsxwriter") as writer:
    for name, df in [("Production", prod_df), ("Engineering", eng_df), ("Design", design_df)]:
        df.to_excel(writer, index=False, sheet_name=name)
        ws = writer.sheets[name]
        ws.set_column(0, 0, 30)
        ws.set_column(1, 1, 12)
        ws.set_column(2, 2, 64)
        ws.set_column(3, 3, 86)
        ws.set_column(4, 4, 80, None, {'hidden': True})
        ws.set_column(5, 7, 14)
        ws.set_column(8, 8, 20)
        ws.freeze_panes(1, 0)
        ws.autofilter(0, 0, len(df), len(df.columns)-1)

    # Build Top 10 by Phase
    t = writer.book.add_worksheet("Top 10 by Phase")
    max_rows = 4000

    def col_to_idx(col):
        col = col.upper()
        n=0
        for ch in col:
            n = n*26 + (ord(ch)-64)
        return n-1

    # Hidden helper columns for each sheet/phase (keys = Score + tie-breaker)
    helpers = [
        ("Production","MVP","BA"), ("Production","Pre-Alpha","BB"), ("Production","Live","BC"),
        ("Engineering","MVP","BD"), ("Engineering","Pre-Alpha","BE"), ("Engineering","Live","BF"),
        ("Design","MVP","BG"), ("Design","Pre-Alpha","BH"), ("Design","Live","BI"),
    ]
    for sheet, phase, col in helpers:
        ci = col_to_idx(col)
        t.write(0, ci, f"{sheet}_{phase}_keys")
        for r in range(2, max_rows+1):
            t.write_formula(r-1, ci, f'=IF(TRIM({sheet}!$B{r})="{phase}", {sheet}!$H{r}+ROW()/{100000}, "")')
        t.set_column(ci, ci, 2, None, {'hidden': True})

    headers = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why — technical","Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner"]
    blocks = [
        ("MVP","Production",0,0,"BA"),       ("MVP","Engineering",0,12,"BD"),       ("MVP","Design",0,24,"BG"),
        ("Pre-Alpha","Production",24,0,"BB"),("Pre-Alpha","Engineering",24,12,"BE"),("Pre-Alpha","Design",24,24,"BH"),
        ("Live","Production",48,0,"BC"),     ("Live","Engineering",48,12,"BF"),     ("Live","Design",48,24,"BI"),
    ]

    for phase, sheet, top, left, key_col in blocks:
        t.write(top, left, f"{phase} — Top 10 ({sheet})")
        for i, h in enumerate(headers):
            t.write(top+1, left+i, h)

        key_rng   = f"${key_col}$2:${key_col}${max_rows}"
        cat_rng   = f"{sheet}!$A$2:$A${max_rows}"
        phs_rng   = f"{sheet}!$B$2:$B${max_rows}"
        risk_rng  = f"{sheet}!$C$2:$C${max_rows}"
        why_rng   = f"{sheet}!$D$2:$D${max_rows}"
        whyt_rng  = f"{sheet}!$E$2:$E${max_rows}"
        like_rng  = f"{sheet}!$F$2:$F${max_rows}"
        imp_rng   = f"{sheet}!$G$2:$G${max_rows}"
        score_rng = f"{sheet}!$H$2:$H${max_rows}"
        own_rng   = f"{sheet}!$I$2:$I${max_rows}"

        # Ten rows per block
        for r_off in range(10):
            rk = f"MATCH(LARGE({key_rng}, ROW($A1)+{r_off}), {key_rng}, 0)"
            base = top+2+r_off
            t.write_formula(base, left+0, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({cat_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+1, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({phs_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+2, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({risk_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+3, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({why_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+4, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({whyt_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+5, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({like_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+6, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({imp_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+7, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({score_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+8, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({own_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")

    # a bit of layout for readability
    t.set_column(0, 0, 28); t.set_column(1, 1, 10); t.set_column(2, 2, 60)
    t.set_column(3, 3, 90); t.set_column(4, 4, 80, None, {'hidden': True})
    t.set_column(5, 7, 14); t.set_column(8, 8, 20)

# Provide download link
display_dataframe_to_user("Download full workbook (3 tabs + 9 Top-10 blocks)", pd.DataFrame({"Download":[out_path]}))

Here’s the full workbook with all **three tabs** and the **9 Top-10 blocks** wired and formula-driven:

**Download:** [Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_ALL_v21_template.xlsx](sandbox:/mnt/data/Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_ALL_v21_template.xlsx)

What’s in it:
- **Production** tab — headers in place, ready for paste.  
- **Engineering** tab — headers in place, ready for paste.  
- **Design** tab — fully populated from our consolidated list.  
- **Top 10 by Phase** — 9 blocks (MVP, Pre-Alpha, Live × Production, Engineering, Design) using LARGE+INDEX/MATCH over hidden helper columns. Once you paste your Production and Engineering rows under the headers, the Top-10 blocks will auto-populate.

Why this version is a “template”:
- I couldn’t access your prior Production/Engineering workbook in this environment, so I didn’t inject stale or guessed data. Paste your latest rows into their respective tabs and you’re set; no further edits to formulas are needed.

import pandas as pd
from caas_jupyter_tools import display_dataframe_to_user

# Canonical columns for all tabs
cols = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why — technical",
        "Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner"]

# ---------------------- PRODUCTION RISKS ----------------------
P = []
def addP(cat, phase, risk, why, whytech, like, imp, owner):
    P.append([cat, phase, risk, why, whytech, like, imp, None, owner])

# Governance & Planning
addP("Governance & Planning","MVP",
     "Single-producer bottleneck",
     "One producer carries roadmap, priorities, comms and approvals; queues build up and decisions stall.",

# ---------------------- WRITE WORKBOOK ----------------------
out_path = "/mnt/data/Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_ALL_v22.xlsx"
with pd.ExcelWriter(out_path, engine="xlsxwriter") as writer:
    for name, df in [("Production", prod_df), ("Engineering", eng_df), ("Design", design_df)]:
        df.to_excel(writer, index=False, sheet_name=name)
        ws = writer.sheets[name]
        ws.set_column(0, 0, 30)
        ws.set_column(1, 1, 12)
        ws.set_column(2, 2, 64)
        ws.set_column(3, 3, 90)
        ws.set_column(4, 4, 70, None, {'hidden': True})
        ws.set_column(5, 7, 14)
        ws.set_column(8, 8, 22)
        ws.freeze_panes(1, 0)
        ws.autofilter(0, 0, len(df), len(df.columns)-1)

    # Build Top 10 by Phase worksheet (9 blocks)
    t = writer.book.add_worksheet("Top 10 by Phase")
    max_rows = 4000

    def col_to_idx(col):
        col = col.upper()
        n=0
        for ch in col:
            n = n*26 + (ord(ch)-64)
        return n-1

    helpers = [
        ("Production","MVP","BA"), ("Production","Pre-Alpha","BB"), ("Production","Live","BC"),
        ("Engineering","MVP","BD"), ("Engineering","Pre-Alpha","BE"), ("Engineering","Live","BF"),
        ("Design","MVP","BG"), ("Design","Pre-Alpha","BH"), ("Design","Live","BI"),
    ]
    # Hidden helper columns create sortable keys: Score + tiny row tiebreaker
    for sheet, phase, col in helpers:
        ci = col_to_idx(col)
        t.write(0, ci, f"{sheet}_{phase}_keys")
        for r in range(2, max_rows+1):
            t.write_formula(r-1, ci, f'=IF(TRIM({sheet}!$B{r})="{phase}", {sheet}!$H{r}+ROW()/{100000}, "")')
        t.set_column(ci, ci, 2, None, {'hidden': True})

    headers = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why — technical","Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner"]
    blocks = [
        ("MVP","Production",0,0,"BA"),       ("MVP","Engineering",0,12,"BD"),       ("MVP","Design",0,24,"BG"),
        ("Pre-Alpha","Production",24,0,"BB"),("Pre-Alpha","Engineering",24,12,"BE"),("Pre-Alpha","Design",24,24,"BH"),
        ("Live","Production",48,0,"BC"),     ("Live","Engineering",48,12,"BF"),     ("Live","Design",48,24,"BI"),
    ]

    for phase, sheet, top, left, key_col in blocks:
        t.write(top, left, f"{phase} — Top 10 ({sheet})")
        for i, h in enumerate(headers):
            t.write(top+1, left+i, h)

        key_rng   = f"${key_col}$2:${key_col}${max_rows}"
        cat_rng   = f"{sheet}!$A$2:$A${max_rows}"
        phs_rng   = f"{sheet}!$B$2:$B${max_rows}"
        risk_rng  = f"{sheet}!$C$2:$C${max_rows}"
        why_rng   = f"{sheet}!$D$2:$D${max_rows}"
        whyt_rng  = f"{sheet}!$E$2:$E${max_rows}"
        like_rng  = f"{sheet}!$F$2:$F${max_rows}"
        imp_rng   = f"{sheet}!$G$2:$G${max_rows}"
        score_rng = f"{sheet}!$H$2:$H${max_rows}"
        own_rng   = f"{sheet}!$I$2:$I${max_rows}"

        for r_off in range(10):
            rk = f"MATCH(LARGE({key_rng}, ROW($A1)+{r_off}), {key_rng}, 0)"
            base = top+2+r_off
            t.write_formula(base, left+0, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({cat_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+1, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({phs_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+2, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({risk_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+3, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({why_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+4, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({whyt_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+5, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({like_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+6, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({imp_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+7, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({score_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+8, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({own_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")

    t.set_column(0, 0, 28); t.set_column(1, 1, 10); t.set_column(2, 2, 60)
    t.set_column(3, 3, 90); t.set_column(4, 4, 70, None, {'hidden': True})
    t.set_column(5, 7, 14); t.set_column(8, 8, 22)

# Present link
display_dataframe_to_user("Workbook with Production, Engineering, Design + 9 Top-10 blocks (v22)", 
                          pd.DataFrame({"Download":[out_path]}))

import pandas as pd
from caas_jupyter_tools import display_dataframe_to_user

cols = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why — technical",
        "Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner"]

prod_df = pd.DataFrame(P, columns=cols)
prod_df["Likelihood (1-10)"] = pd.to_numeric(prod_df["Likelihood (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
prod_df["Impact (1-10)"] = pd.to_numeric(prod_df["Impact (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
prod_df["Risk Score (LxI)"] = prod_df["Likelihood (1-10)"] * prod_df["Impact (1-10)"]

eng_df  = pd.DataFrame(E, columns=cols)
eng_df["Likelihood (1-10)"] = pd.to_numeric(eng_df["Likelihood (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
eng_df["Impact (1-10)"] = pd.to_numeric(eng_df["Impact (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
eng_df["Risk Score (LxI)"] = eng_df["Likelihood (1-10)"] * eng_df["Impact (1-10)"]

# Reuse the Design DF from previous cell: reconstruct succinctly by copying prod structure and replacing
design_rows = [row[:] for row in P[:0]]  # empty template
# For brevity, include a subset of highest-signal Design items; can be expanded if needed
design_sample = [
("Core Loop & Vision","MVP","Core loop not uniformly defined across teams",
 "Different teams interpret the core experience differently and ship features that do not reinforce one another.",
 "No single-page Core Loop spec with verbs, cadence, rewards, anti-goals and success criteria approved and versioned; features reference different assumptions.",
 9,9,"Lead Designer"),
("Design–Engineering Contract","MVP","Design specs do not translate to buildable work",
 "Features ship half-shaped or drift after handoff.",
 "No RFC template with acceptance tests and performance targets per feature.",
 8,8,"Tech Designer"),
("Content Scope & Depth","MVP","Breadth over depth for Investor MVP",
 "Teams try to show many systems at once; nothing feels complete or sticky.",
 "No razor for the first 30 minutes; slice lacks depth KPIs; feature briefs do not include 'what is intentionally missing' cuts.",
 8,8,"Game Director"),
("Economy & Rewards","MVP","Reward inflation or drought",
 "Players either drown in rewards or feel unrewarded and churn.",
 "No source/sink model; drop-rate tables and daily caps missing; sink cost curves not defined.",
 8,9,"Economy Designer"),
("Onboarding & UX","MVP","Onboarding fails to teach the loop",
 "Players do not grasp what to do or why; bounce early.",
 "No scripted FTUE path with success criteria; no instrumentation to see where players drop.",
 7,8,"UX Designer"),
("Content Lock","MVP","Content lock discipline not enforced for Investor MVP",
 "Scope creep undermines demo stability.",
 "No lock calendar, change-control or demo-safe checklist.",
 8,9,"Design Producer"),
("Playtesting","MVP","Insufficient structured playtests",
 "Blind spots persist into public builds.",
 "No weekly playtest scripts, goals and triage loop owned by design.",
 7,7,"Design Producer"),
("Design Leadership & Governance","MVP","Design leadership bandwidth is over-stretched",
 "Many juniors need review while few senior designers can approve.",
 "High review and mentoring load on a small set of leads creates long queues; briefs and gates stall.",
 8,8,"Game Director"),

design_df = pd.DataFrame(design_sample, columns=cols)
design_df["Risk Score (LxI)"] = pd.to_numeric(design_df["Likelihood (1-10)"]) * pd.to_numeric(design_df["Impact (1-10)"])

out_path = "/mnt/data/Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_ALL_v22_MIN.xlsx"

with pd.ExcelWriter(out_path, engine="xlsxwriter") as writer:
    for name, df in [("Production", prod_df), ("Engineering", eng_df), ("Design", design_df)]:
        df.to_excel(writer, index=False, sheet_name=name)
        ws = writer.sheets[name]
        ws.set_column(0, 0, 30)
        ws.set_column(1, 1, 12)
        ws.set_column(2, 2, 64)
        ws.set_column(3, 3, 90)
        ws.set_column(4, 4, 70, None, {'hidden': True})
        ws.set_column(5, 7, 14)
        ws.set_column(8, 8, 22)
        ws.freeze_panes(1, 0)
        ws.autofilter(0, 0, len(df), len(df.columns)-1)

    # Build Top 10 by Phase worksheet (9 blocks)
    t = writer.book.add_worksheet("Top 10 by Phase")
    max_rows = 4000

    def col_to_idx(col):
        col = col.upper()
        n=0
        for ch in col:
            n = n*26 + (ord(ch)-64)
        return n-1

    helpers = [
        ("Production","MVP","BA"), ("Production","Pre-Alpha","BB"), ("Production","Live","BC"),
        ("Engineering","MVP","BD"), ("Engineering","Pre-Alpha","BE"), ("Engineering","Live","BF"),
        ("Design","MVP","BG"), ("Design","Pre-Alpha","BH"), ("Design","Live","BI"),
    ]
    for sheet, phase, col in helpers:
        ci = col_to_idx(col)
        t.write(0, ci, f"{sheet}_{phase}_keys")
        for r in range(2, max_rows+1):
            t.write_formula(r-1, ci, f'=IF(TRIM({sheet}!$B{r})="{phase}", {sheet}!$H{r}+ROW()/{100000}, "")')
        t.set_column(ci, ci, 2, None, {'hidden': True})

    headers = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why — technical","Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner"]
    blocks = [
        ("MVP","Production",0,0,"BA"),       ("MVP","Engineering",0,12,"BD"),       ("MVP","Design",0,24,"BG"),
        ("Pre-Alpha","Production",24,0,"BB"),("Pre-Alpha","Engineering",24,12,"BE"),("Pre-Alpha","Design",24,24,"BH"),
        ("Live","Production",48,0,"BC"),     ("Live","Engineering",48,12,"BF"),     ("Live","Design",48,24,"BI"),
    ]

    for phase, sheet, top, left, key_col in blocks:
        t.write(top, left, f"{phase} — Top 10 ({sheet})")
        for i, h in enumerate(headers):
            t.write(top+1, left+i, h)

        key_rng   = f"${key_col}$2:${key_col}${max_rows}"
        ranges = {
            "cat":   f"{sheet}!$A$2:$A${max_rows}",
            "phs":   f"{sheet}!$B$2:$B${max_rows}",
            "risk":  f"{sheet}!$C$2:$C${max_rows}",
            "why":   f"{sheet}!$D$2:$D${max_rows}",
            "whyt":  f"{sheet}!$E$2:$E${max_rows}",
            "like":  f"{sheet}!$F$2:$F${max_rows}",
            "imp":   f"{sheet}!$G$2:$G${max_rows}",
            "score": f"{sheet}!$H$2:$H${max_rows}",
            "own":   f"{sheet}!$I$2:$I${max_rows}",
        }
        for r_off in range(10):
            rk = f"MATCH(LARGE({key_rng}, ROW($A1)+{r_off}), {key_rng}, 0)"
            base = top+2+r_off
            t.write_formula(base, left+0, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({ranges['cat']}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+1, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({ranges['phs']}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+2, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({ranges['risk']}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+3, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({ranges['why']}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+4, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({ranges['whyt']}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+5, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({ranges['like']}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+6, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({ranges['imp']}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+7, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({ranges['score']}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+8, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({ranges['own']}, {rk}), \"\")")

    t.set_column(0, 0, 28); t.set_column(1, 1, 10); t.set_column(2, 2, 60)
    t.set_column(3, 3, 90); t.set_column(4, 4, 70, None, {'hidden': True})
    t.set_column(5, 7, 14); t.set_column(8, 8, 22)

import pandas as pd
from caas_jupyter_tools import display_dataframe_to_user

# Reuse P and E from previous cells
cols = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why — technical",
        "Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner"]

prod_df = pd.DataFrame(P, columns=cols)
prod_df["Likelihood (1-10)"] = pd.to_numeric(prod_df["Likelihood (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
prod_df["Impact (1-10)"] = pd.to_numeric(prod_df["Impact (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
prod_df["Risk Score (LxI)"] = prod_df["Likelihood (1-10)"] * prod_df["Impact (1-10)"]

eng_df  = pd.DataFrame(E, columns=cols)
eng_df["Likelihood (1-10)"] = pd.to_numeric(eng_df["Likelihood (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
eng_df["Impact (1-10)"] = pd.to_numeric(eng_df["Impact (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
eng_df["Risk Score (LxI)"] = eng_df["Likelihood (1-10)"] * eng_df["Impact (1-10)"]

# Fix design sample rows to include placeholder for Risk Score column
design_sample = [
("Core Loop & Vision","MVP","Core loop not uniformly defined across teams",
 "Different teams interpret the core experience differently and ship features that do not reinforce one another.",
 "No single-page Core Loop spec with verbs, cadence, rewards, anti-goals and success criteria approved and versioned; features reference different assumptions.",
 9,9,None,"Lead Designer"),
("Design–Engineering Contract","MVP","Design specs do not translate to buildable work",
 "Features ship half-shaped or drift after handoff.",
 "No RFC template with acceptance tests and performance targets per feature.",
 8,8,None,"Tech Designer"),
("Content Scope & Depth","MVP","Breadth over depth for Investor MVP",

 8,8,None,"Game Director"),
("Economy & Rewards","MVP","Reward inflation or drought",

 "No source/sink model; drop-rate tables and daily caps missing; sink cost curves not defined.",

("Onboarding & UX","MVP","Onboarding fails to teach the loop",

("Design Leadership & Governance","MVP","Design leadership bandwidth is over-stretched",

out_path = "/mnt/data/Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_ALL_v23.xlsx"
with pd.ExcelWriter(out_path, engine="xlsxwriter") as writer:
    for name, df in [("Production", prod_df), ("Engineering", eng_df), ("Design", design_df)]:
        df.to_excel(writer, index=False, sheet_name=name)
        ws = writer.sheets[name]
        ws.set_column(0, 0, 30)
        ws.set_column(1, 1, 12)
        ws.set_column(2, 2, 64)
        ws.set_column(3, 3, 90)
        ws.set_column(4, 4, 70, None, {'hidden': True})
        ws.set_column(5, 7, 14)
        ws.set_column(8, 8, 22)
        ws.freeze_panes(1, 0)
        ws.autofilter(0, 0, len(df), len(df.columns)-1)

    # Top 10 by Phase
    t = writer.book.add_worksheet("Top 10 by Phase")
    max_rows = 4000

    def col_to_idx(col):
        col = col.upper()
        n=0
        for ch in col:
            n = n*26 + (ord(ch)-64)
        return n-1

    helpers = [
        ("Production","MVP","BA"), ("Production","Pre-Alpha","BB"), ("Production","Live","BC"),
        ("Engineering","MVP","BD"), ("Engineering","Pre-Alpha","BE"), ("Engineering","Live","BF"),
        ("Design","MVP","BG"), ("Design","Pre-Alpha","BH"), ("Design","Live","BI"),
    ]
    for sheet, phase, col in helpers:
        ci = col_to_idx(col)
        t.write(0, ci, f"{sheet}_{phase}_keys")
        for r in range(2, max_rows+1):
            t.write_formula(r-1, ci, f'=IF(TRIM({sheet}!$B{r})="{phase}", {sheet}!$H{r}+ROW()/{100000}, "")')
        t.set_column(ci, ci, 2, None, {'hidden': True})

    headers = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why — technical","Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner"]
    blocks = [
        ("MVP","Production",0,0,"BA"),       ("MVP","Engineering",0,12,"BD"),       ("MVP","Design",0,24,"BG"),
        ("Pre-Alpha","Production",24,0,"BB"),("Pre-Alpha","Engineering",24,12,"BE"),("Pre-Alpha","Design",24,24,"BH"),
        ("Live","Production",48,0,"BC"),     ("Live","Engineering",48,12,"BF"),     ("Live","Design",48,24,"BI"),
    ]

    for phase, sheet, top, left, key_col in blocks:
        t.write(top, left, f"{phase} — Top 10 ({sheet})")
        for i, h in enumerate(headers):
            t.write(top+1, left+i, h)

        key_rng   = f"${key_col}$2:${key_col}${max_rows}"
        cat_rng   = f"{sheet}!$A$2:$A${max_rows}"
        phs_rng   = f"{sheet}!$B$2:$B${max_rows}"
        risk_rng  = f"{sheet}!$C$2:$C${max_rows}"
        why_rng   = f"{sheet}!$D$2:$D${max_rows}"
        whyt_rng  = f"{sheet}!$E$2:$E${max_rows}"
        like_rng  = f"{sheet}!$F$2:$F${max_rows}"
        imp_rng   = f"{sheet}!$G$2:$G${max_rows}"
        score_rng = f"{sheet}!$H$2:$H${max_rows}"
        own_rng   = f"{sheet}!$I$2:$I${max_rows}"

        for r_off in range(10):
            rk = f"MATCH(LARGE({key_rng}, ROW($A1)+{r_off}), {key_rng}, 0)"
            base = top+2+r_off
            t.write_formula(base, left+0, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({cat_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+1, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({phs_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+2, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({risk_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+3, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({why_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+4, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({whyt_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+5, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({like_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+6, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({imp_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+7, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({score_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+8, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({own_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")

    t.set_column(0, 0, 28); t.set_column(1, 1, 10); t.set_column(2, 2, 60)
    t.set_column(3, 3, 90); t.set_column(4, 4, 70, None, {'hidden': True})
    t.set_column(5, 7, 14); t.set_column(8, 8, 22)

display_dataframe_to_user("Download: Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_ALL_v23.xlsx",
                          pd.DataFrame({"Download":["/mnt/data/Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_ALL_v23.xlsx"],

with pd.ExcelWriter(out_path, engine="xlsxwriter") as writer:
    for name, df in [("Production", prod_df), ("Engineering", eng_df), ("Design", design_df)]:
        df.to_excel(writer, index=False, sheet_name=name)
        ws = writer.sheets[name]
        ws.set_column(0, 0, 30)
        ws.set_column(1, 1, 12)
        ws.set_column(2, 2, 64)
        ws.set_column(3, 3, 92)
        ws.set_column(4, 4, 72, None, {'hidden': True})
        ws.set_column(5, 7, 14)
        ws.set_column(8, 8, 24)
        ws.freeze_panes(1, 0)
        ws.autofilter(0, 0, len(df), len(df.columns)-1)

    # Top 10 by Phase worksheet (9 blocks)
    t = writer.book.add_worksheet("Top 10 by Phase")
    max_rows = 4000

    def col_to_idx(col):
        col = col.upper()
        n=0
        for ch in col:
            n = n*26 + (ord(ch)-64)
        return n-1

    helpers = [
        ("Production","MVP","BA"), ("Production","Pre-Alpha","BB"), ("Production","Live","BC"),
        ("Engineering","MVP","BD"), ("Engineering","Pre-Alpha","BE"), ("Engineering","Live","BF"),
        ("Design","MVP","BG"), ("Design","Pre-Alpha","BH"), ("Design","Live","BI"),
    ]
    # Hidden helper columns compute a sortable key: Risk Score + tiny row tiebreaker
    for sheet, phase, col in helpers:
        ci = col_to_idx(col)
        t.write(0, ci, f"{sheet}_{phase}_keys")
        for r in range(2, max_rows+1):
            t.write_formula(r-1, ci, f'=IF(TRIM({sheet}!$B{r})="{phase}", {sheet}!$H{r}+ROW()/{100000}, "")')
        t.set_column(ci, ci, 2, None, {'hidden': True})

    headers = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why — technical","Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner"]
    blocks = [
        ("MVP","Production",0,0,"BA"),       ("MVP","Engineering",0,12,"BD"),       ("MVP","Design",0,24,"BG"),
        ("Pre-Alpha","Production",24,0,"BB"),("Pre-Alpha","Engineering",24,12,"BE"),("Pre-Alpha","Design",24,24,"BH"),
        ("Live","Production",48,0,"BC"),     ("Live","Engineering",48,12,"BF"),     ("Live","Design",48,24,"BI"),
    ]

    for phase, sheet, top, left, key_col in blocks:
        t.write(top, left, f"{phase} — Top 10 ({sheet})")
        for i, h in enumerate(headers):
            t.write(top+1, left+i, h)

        key_rng   = f"${key_col}$2:${key_col}${max_rows}"
        cat_rng   = f"{sheet}!$A$2:$A${max_rows}"
        phs_rng   = f"{sheet}!$B$2:$B${max_rows}"
        risk_rng  = f"{sheet}!$C$2:$C${max_rows}"
        why_rng   = f"{sheet}!$D$2:$D${max_rows}"
        whyt_rng  = f"{sheet}!$E$2:$E${max_rows}"
        like_rng  = f"{sheet}!$F$2:$F${max_rows}"
        imp_rng   = f"{sheet}!$G$2:$G${max_rows}"
        score_rng = f"{sheet}!$H$2:$H${max_rows}"
        own_rng   = f"{sheet}!$I$2:$I${max_rows}"

        for r_off in range(10):
            rk = f"MATCH(LARGE({key_rng}, ROW($A1)+{r_off}), {key_rng}, 0)"
            base = top+2+r_off
            t.write_formula(base, left+0, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({cat_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+1, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({phs_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+2, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({risk_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+3, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({why_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+4, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({whyt_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+5, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({like_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+6, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({imp_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+7, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({score_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+8, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({own_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")

    t.set_column(0, 0, 28); t.set_column(1, 1, 10); t.set_column(2, 2, 60)
    t.set_column(3, 3, 92); t.set_column(4, 4, 72, None, {'hidden': True})
    t.set_column(5, 7, 14); t.set_column(8, 8, 24)

display_dataframe_to_user("Download: Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_ALL_v24.xlsx",
                          pd.DataFrame({"Download":[out_path],
                                        "Rows":[f"Production={len(prod_df)}, Engineering={len(eng_df)}, Design={len(design_df)}"]}))

# Add the requested 'Valeria' column to capture her feedback
def with_valeria(df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
    out = df.copy()
    if "Valeria" not in out.columns:
        out["Valeria"] = ""
    return out

            t.write(top+1, left+i, h)

        key_rng   = f"${key_col}$2:${key_col}${max_rows}"
        cat_rng   = f"{sheet}!$A$2:$A${max_rows}"
        phs_rng   = f"{sheet}!$B$2:$B${max_rows}"
        risk_rng  = f"{sheet}!$C$2:$C${max_rows}"
        why_rng   = f"{sheet}!$D$2:$D${max_rows}"
        whyt_rng  = f"{sheet}!$E$2:$E${max_rows}"
        like_rng  = f"{sheet}!$F$2:$F${max_rows}"
        imp_rng   = f"{sheet}!$G$2:$G${max_rows}"
        score_rng = f"{sheet}!$H$2:$H${max_rows}"
        own_rng   = f"{sheet}!$I$2:$I${max_rows}"

        for r_off in range(10):
            rk = f"MATCH(LARGE({key_rng}, ROW($A1)+{r_off}), {key_rng}, 0)"
            base = top+2+r_off
            t.write_formula(base, left+0, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({cat_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+1, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({phs_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+2, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({risk_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+3, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({why_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+4, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({whyt_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+5, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({like_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+6, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({imp_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+7, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({score_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+8, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({own_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")

    t.set_column(0, 0, 28); t.set_column(1, 1, 10); t.set_column(2, 2, 60)
    t.set_column(3, 3, 92); t.set_column(4, 4, 72, None, {'hidden': True})

import pandas as pd
from caas_jupyter_tools import display_dataframe_to_user

# Utility to ensure column naming matches the no–em-dash rule
def normalise_cols(df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
    out = df.copy()
    if "Why — technical" in out.columns:
        out = out.rename(columns={"Why — technical": "Why (technical)"})
    return out

# 1) Start from the last delivered dataframes if present
try:
    prod_df = normalise_cols(prod_df)
    eng_df  = normalise_cols(eng_df)
    design_df = normalise_cols(design_df)
except NameError:
    raise RuntimeError("Source dataframes not found from prior step; cannot diff.")

# Canonical column order
COLS = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why (technical)",
        "Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner"]

def ensure_cols(df):
    # Add Risk Score if missing
    out = df.copy()
    if "Risk Score (LxI)" not in out.columns:
        out["Risk Score (LxI)"] = pd.to_numeric(out["Likelihood (1-10)"], errors="coerce") * pd.to_numeric(out["Impact (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
    # Add Valeria column if not there; we'll append it later to all
    missing = [c for c in COLS if c not in out.columns]
    for c in missing:
        out[c] = "" if c not in ["Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)"] else 0
    return out[COLS]

prod_df = ensure_cols(prod_df)
eng_df  = ensure_cols(eng_df)
design_df = ensure_cols(design_df)

# Helper to append new rows
def add_rows(df, rows):
    add_df = pd.DataFrame(rows, columns=COLS)
    add_df["Likelihood (1-10)"] = pd.to_numeric(add_df["Likelihood (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
    add_df["Impact (1-10)"] = pd.to_numeric(add_df["Impact (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
    add_df["Risk Score (LxI)"] = add_df["Likelihood (1-10)"] * add_df["Impact (1-10)"]
    return pd.concat([df, add_df], ignore_index=True)

# Build change log by comparing risk names vs previous versions
def diff_names(old_df, new_df, label):
    old = set(old_df["Risk"].tolist())
    new = set(new_df["Risk"].tolist())
    added = sorted(list(new - old))
    removed = sorted(list(old - new))
    return pd.DataFrame({
        "Area":[label]*max(len(added),1),
        "Added":[", ".join(added) if added else ""],
        "Removed":[", ".join(removed) if removed else ""],
        "New Count":[len(new)]
    })

change_log = pd.concat([
    diff_names(prod_df, prod_full, "Production"),
    diff_names(eng_df, eng_full, "Engineering"),
    diff_names(design_df, design_full, "Design")
], ignore_index=True)

        ws = writer.sheets[name]
        ws.set_column(0, 0, 30)
        ws.set_column(1, 1, 12)

        ws.set_column(3, 3, 92)
        ws.set_column(4, 4, 72, None, {'hidden': True})
        ws.set_column(5, 7, 14)
        ws.set_column(8, 8, 24)
        if "Valeria" in df.columns:
            ws.set_column(9, 9, 32)
        ws.freeze_panes(1, 0)
        ws.autofilter(0, 0, len(df), len(df.columns)-1)

    # Top 10 by Phase
    t = writer.book.add_worksheet("Top 10 by Phase")
    max_rows = 10000  # safe upper bound

    def col_to_idx(col):
        col = col.upper()
        n=0
        for ch in col:
            n = n*26 + (ord(ch)-64)
        return n-1

    helpers = [
        ("Production","MVP","BA"), ("Production","Pre-Alpha","BB"), ("Production","Live","BC"),
        ("Engineering","MVP","BD"), ("Engineering","Pre-Alpha","BE"), ("Engineering","Live","BF"),
        ("Design","MVP","BG"), ("Design","Pre-Alpha","BH"), ("Design","Live","BI"),
    ]
    for sheet, phase, col in helpers:
        ci = col_to_idx(col)
        t.write(0, ci, f"{sheet}_{phase}_keys")
        for r in range(2, max_rows+1):
            t.write_formula(r-1, ci, f'=IF(TRIM({sheet}!$B{r})="{phase}", {sheet}!$H{r}+ROW()/{100000}, "")')
        t.set_column(ci, ci, 2, None, {'hidden': True})

    headers = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why (technical)","Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner"]
    blocks = [
        ("MVP","Production",0,0,"BA"),       ("MVP","Engineering",0,12,"BD"),       ("MVP","Design",0,24,"BG"),

    ]
    for phase, sheet, top, left, key_col in blocks:
        t.write(top, left, f"{phase} Top 10 — {sheet}")
        for i, h in enumerate(headers):
            t.write(top+1, left+i, h)

        key_rng   = f"${key_col}$2:${key_col}${max_rows}"
        rngs = {
            "cat":   f"{sheet}!$A$2:$A${max_rows}",
            "phs":   f"{sheet}!$B$2:$B${max_rows}",
            "risk":  f"{sheet}!$C$2:$C${max_rows}",
            "why":   f"{sheet}!$D$2:$D${max_rows}",
            "whyt":  f"{sheet}!$E$2:$E${max_rows}",
            "like":  f"{sheet}!$F$2:$F${max_rows}",
            "imp":   f"{sheet}!$G$2:$G${max_rows}",
            "score": f"{sheet}!$H$2:$H${max_rows}",
            "own":   f"{sheet}!$I$2:$I${max_rows}",

        for r_off in range(10):

            t.write_formula(base, left+8, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({rngs['own']}, {rk}), \"\")")

import pandas as pd
from caas_jupyter_tools import display_dataframe_to_user

# Retry build with fixed change log and no em dashes anywhere
def normalise_cols(df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
    out = df.copy()
    if "Why — technical" in out.columns:
        out = out.rename(columns={"Why — technical": "Why (technical)"})
    return out

try:
    prod_df = normalise_cols(prod_df)
    eng_df  = normalise_cols(eng_df)
    design_df = normalise_cols(design_df)
except NameError:
    raise RuntimeError("Source dataframes not found from prior step; cannot diff.")

COLS = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why (technical)",
        "Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner"]

def ensure_cols(df):
    out = df.copy()
    if "Risk Score (LxI)" not in out.columns:
        out["Risk Score (LxI)"] = pd.to_numeric(out["Likelihood (1-10)"], errors="coerce") * pd.to_numeric(out["Impact (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
    for c in COLS:
        if c not in out.columns:
            out[c] = "" if c not in ["Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)"] else 0
    return out[COLS]

prod_df = ensure_cols(prod_df)
eng_df  = ensure_cols(eng_df)
design_df = ensure_cols(design_df)

def add_rows(df, rows):
    add_df = pd.DataFrame(rows, columns=COLS)
    add_df["Likelihood (1-10)"] = pd.to_numeric(add_df["Likelihood (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
    add_df["Impact (1-10)"] = pd.to_numeric(add_df["Impact (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
    add_df["Risk Score (LxI)"] = add_df["Likelihood (1-10)"] * add_df["Impact (1-10)"]
    return pd.concat([df, add_df], ignore_index=True)

# One-row change log per area
def diff_row(old_df, new_df, label):
    old = set(old_df["Risk"].tolist())
    new = set(new_df["Risk"].tolist())
    added = sorted(list(new - old))
    removed = sorted(list(old - new))
    return pd.DataFrame([{
        "Area": label,
        "Added": "; ".join(added),
        "Removed": "; ".join(removed),
        "New Count": len(new)
    }])

change_log = pd.concat([
    diff_row(prod_df, prod_full, "Production"),
    diff_row(eng_df, eng_full, "Engineering"),
    diff_row(design_df, design_full, "Design")
], ignore_index=True)

with pd.ExcelWriter(out_path, engine="xlsxwriter") as writer:
    for name, df in [("Production", prod_full), ("Engineering", eng_full), ("Design", design_full)]:
        cols_out = COLS + ["Valeria"]
        df = df[cols_out]
        df.to_excel(writer, index=False, sheet_name=name)
        ws = writer.sheets[name]
        ws.set_column(0, 0, 30)
        ws.set_column(1, 1, 12)
        ws.set_column(2, 2, 64)
        ws.set_column(3, 3, 92)
        ws.set_column(4, 4, 72, None, {'hidden': True})
        ws.set_column(5, 7, 14)
        ws.set_column(8, 8, 24)
        ws.set_column(9, 9, 32)  # Valeria
        ws.freeze_panes(1, 0)
        ws.autofilter(0, 0, len(df), len(df.columns)-1)

    # Top 10 by Phase
    t = writer.book.add_worksheet("Top 10 by Phase")
    max_rows = 10000

    def col_to_idx(col):
        col = col.upper()
        n=0
        for ch in col:
            n = n*26 + (ord(ch)-64)
        return n-1

    helpers = [
        ("Production","MVP","BA"), ("Production","Pre-Alpha","BB"), ("Production","Live","BC"),
        ("Engineering","MVP","BD"), ("Engineering","Pre-Alpha","BE"), ("Engineering","Live","BF"),
        ("Design","MVP","BG"), ("Design","Pre-Alpha","BH"), ("Design","Live","BI"),
    ]
    for sheet, phase, col in helpers:
        ci = col_to_idx(col)
        t.write(0, ci, f"{sheet}_{phase}_keys")
        for r in range(2, max_rows+1):
            t.write_formula(r-1, ci, f'=IF(TRIM({sheet}!$B{r})="{phase}", {sheet}!$H{r}+ROW()/{100000}, "")')
        t.set_column(ci, ci, 2, None, {'hidden': True})

    headers = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why (technical)","Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner"]
    blocks = [
        ("MVP","Production",0,0,"BA"),       ("MVP","Engineering",0,12,"BD"),       ("MVP","Design",0,24,"BG"),
        ("Pre-Alpha","Production",24,0,"BB"),("Pre-Alpha","Engineering",24,12,"BE"),("Pre-Alpha","Design",24,24,"BH"),
        ("Live","Production",48,0,"BC"),     ("Live","Engineering",48,12,"BF"),     ("Live","Design",48,24,"BI"),
    ]
    for phase, sheet, top, left, key_col in blocks:
        t.write(top, left, f"{phase} Top 10 - {sheet}")
        for i, h in enumerate(headers):
            t.write(top+1, left+i, h)

        key_rng   = f"${key_col}$2:${key_col}${max_rows}"
        rngs = {
            "cat":   f"{sheet}!$A$2:$A${max_rows}",
            "phs":   f"{sheet}!$B$2:$B${max_rows}",
            "risk":  f"{sheet}!$C$2:$C${max_rows}",
            "why":   f"{sheet}!$D$2:$D${max_rows}",
            "whyt":  f"{sheet}!$E$2:$E${max_rows}",
            "like":  f"{sheet}!$F$2:$F${max_rows}",
            "imp":   f"{sheet}!$G$2:$G${max_rows}",
            "score": f"{sheet}!$H$2:$H${max_rows}",
            "own":   f"{sheet}!$I$2:$I${max_rows}",
        }
        for r_off in range(10):
            rk = f"MATCH(LARGE({key_rng}, ROW($A1)+{r_off}), {key_rng}, 0)"
            base = top+2+r_off
            t.write_formula(base, left+0, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({rngs['cat']}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+1, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({rngs['phs']}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+2, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({rngs['risk']}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+3, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({rngs['why']}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+4, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({rngs['whyt']}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+5, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({rngs['like']}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+6, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({rngs['imp']}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+7, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({rngs['score']}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+8, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({rngs['own']}, {rk}), \"\")")

    # Change Log (one row per area)
    change_log.to_excel(writer, index=False, sheet_name="Change Log")
