import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from caas_jupyter_tools import display_dataframe_to_user

# === Helper: sanitize text to avoid forbidden punctuation (no em dashes) ===
def sanitize_text(s):
    if pd.isna(s):
        return s
    if not isinstance(s, str):
        s = str(s)
    return s.replace("—", "-").replace("–", "-")

def sanitize_df(df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
    out = df.copy()
    out = out.applymap(sanitize_text)
    return out

# === Pull latest in-memory dataframes; if unavailable, fail fast ===
try:
    prod_full
    eng_full
    design_full
except NameError as e:
    raise RuntimeError("Source tables are not present in the session. I cannot restore without them.") from e

# === Standardize columns & compute Risk Score ===
STD_COLS = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why (technical)",
            "Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner","Valeria"]

def standardise(df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
    d = df.copy()
    # Normalize column names that might differ
    d = d.rename(columns={
        "Why — technical": "Why (technical)",
        "Why- technical": "Why (technical)",
        "Why - technical": "Why (technical)",
        "Risk Score": "Risk Score (LxI)",
        "Risk Score(LxI)": "Risk Score (LxI)"
    })
    # Add missing columns
    for col in STD_COLS:
        if col not in d.columns:
            d[col] = np.nan if col in ["Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)"] else ""
    # Ensure numeric L, I, Score
    d["Likelihood (1-10)"] = pd.to_numeric(d["Likelihood (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
    d["Impact (1-10)"] = pd.to_numeric(d["Impact (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
    # Compute Risk Score if blank
    need_score = d["Risk Score (LxI)"].isna() | (d["Risk Score (LxI)"]=="") | (d["Risk Score (LxI)"]==0)
    d.loc[need_score, "Risk Score (LxI)"] = d["Likelihood (1-10)"] * d["Impact (1-10)"]
    # Add Valeria col if missing
    if "Valeria" not in d.columns:
        d["Valeria"] = ""
    # Reorder
    d = d[STD_COLS]
    # Sanitize punctuation
    d = sanitize_df(d)
    return d

prod_std = standardise(prod_full)
eng_std  = standardise(eng_full)
design_std = standardise(design_full)

# === DO NOT DEDUPLICATE: keep all rows intact ===
# Sort for consistency: by Category, Phase, Risk
prod_std = prod_std.sort_values(["Category","Phase","Risk"], kind="stable").reset_index(drop=True)
eng_std  = eng_std.sort_values(["Category","Phase","Risk"], kind="stable").reset_index(drop=True)
design_std = design_std.sort_values(["Category","Phase","Risk"], kind="stable").reset_index(drop=True)

# === Write restored workbook ===
out_path = "/mnt/data/Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_ALL_v27_RESTORED.xlsx"
with pd.ExcelWriter(out_path, engine="xlsxwriter") as writer:
    for name, df in [("Production", prod_std), ("Engineering", eng_std), ("Design", design_std)]:
        df.to_excel(writer, index=False, sheet_name=name)
        ws = writer.sheets[name]
        # Column widths, no hidden columns
        ws.set_column(0, 0, 26)   # Category
        ws.set_column(1, 1, 12)   # Phase
        ws.set_column(2, 2, 68)   # Risk
        ws.set_column(3, 3, 90)   # Why it would occur
        ws.set_column(4, 4, 80)   # Why (technical)
        ws.set_column(5, 7, 14)   # Likelihood, Impact, Score
        ws.set_column(8, 8, 22)   # Owner
        ws.set_column(9, 9, 28)   # Valeria
        ws.freeze_panes(1, 0)
        ws.autofilter(0, 0, len(df), len(df.columns)-1)

    # Top 10 by Phase — robust classic approach (helper keys + INDEX/MATCH), no dynamic arrays
    t = writer.book.add_worksheet("Top 10 by Phase")
    max_rows = 20000  # large upper bound

    # Helper columns BA..BI for keys per area/phase
    helpers = [
        ("Production","MVP","BA"), ("Production","Pre-Alpha","BB"), ("Production","Live","BC"),
        ("Engineering","MVP","BD"), ("Engineering","Pre-Alpha","BE"), ("Engineering","Live","BF"),
        ("Design","MVP","BG"), ("Design","Pre-Alpha","BH"), ("Design","Live","BI"),
    ]

    def col_to_idx(col):
        col = col.upper()
        n=0
        for ch in col:
            n = n*26 + (ord(ch)-64)
        return n-1

    for sheet, phase, col in helpers:
        ci = col_to_idx(col)
        t.write(0, ci, f"{sheet}_{phase}_keys")
        for r in range(2, max_rows+1):
            # Key = Risk Score + tiny fraction to break ties, but only for matching Phase
            t.write_formula(r-1, ci, f'=IF(TRIM({sheet}!$B{r})="{phase}", {sheet}!$H{r}+ROW()/{100000}, "")')
        t.set_column(ci, ci, 2, None, {'hidden': True})

    headers = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why (technical)","Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)","Owner","Valeria"]
    blocks = [
        ("MVP","Production",0,0,"BA"),       ("MVP","Engineering",0,13,"BD"),       ("MVP","Design",0,26,"BG"),
        ("Pre-Alpha","Production",25,0,"BB"),("Pre-Alpha","Engineering",25,13,"BE"),("Pre-Alpha","Design",25,26,"BH"),
        ("Live","Production",50,0,"BC"),     ("Live","Engineering",50,13,"BF"),     ("Live","Design",50,26,"BI"),
    ]

    for phase, sheet, top, left, key_col in blocks:
        t.write(top, left, f"{phase} Top 10 - {sheet}")
        for i, h in enumerate(headers):
            t.write(top+1, left+i, h)

        key_rng   = f"${key_col}$2:${key_col}${max_rows}"
        cat_rng   = f"{sheet}!$A$2:$A${max_rows}"
        phs_rng   = f"{sheet}!$B$2:$B${max_rows}"
        risk_rng  = f"{sheet}!$C$2:$C${max_rows}"
        why_rng   = f"{sheet}!$D$2:$D${max_rows}"
        whyt_rng  = f"{sheet}!$E$2:$E${max_rows}"
        like_rng  = f"{sheet}!$F$2:$F${max_rows}"
        imp_rng   = f"{sheet}!$G$2:$G${max_rows}"
        score_rng = f"{sheet}!$H$2:$H${max_rows}"
        own_rng   = f"{sheet}!$I$2:$I${max_rows}"
        val_rng   = f"{sheet}!$J$2:$J${max_rows}"

        for r_off in range(10):
            rk = f"MATCH(LARGE({key_rng}, ROW($A1)+{r_off}), {key_rng}, 0)"
            base = top+2+r_off
            t.write_formula(base, left+0, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({cat_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+1, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({phs_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+2, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({risk_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+3, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({why_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+4, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({whyt_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+5, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({like_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+6, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({imp_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+7, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({score_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+8, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({own_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")
            t.write_formula(base, left+9, f"=IFERROR(INDEX({val_rng}, {rk}), \"\")")

# Provide link and quick counts for verification
summary = pd.DataFrame({
    "Sheet": ["Production","Engineering","Design"],
    "Rows": [len(prod_std), len(eng_std), len(design_std)]
})
display_dataframe_to_user("Download: Couch_Heroes_Risk_Register_ALL_v27_RESTORED.xlsx",
                          pd.DataFrame({"Download":[out_path]}))
display_dataframe_to_user("Row counts in v27", summary)

import pandas as pd
from caas_jupyter_tools import display_dataframe_to_user

# Use latest restored dataframes if available; fall back to previous but drop unwanted columns
try:
    prod_std, eng_std, design_std
except NameError:
    raise RuntimeError("Source data not available to rebuild without Owner/Valeria.")

KEEP_COLS = ["Category","Phase","Risk","Why it would occur","Why (technical)",
             "Likelihood (1-10)","Impact (1-10)","Risk Score (LxI)"]

def trim_cols(df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
    out = df.copy()
    # Recompute Risk Score to be safe
    out["Likelihood (1-10)"] = pd.to_numeric(out["Likelihood (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
    out["Impact (1-10)"] = pd.to_numeric(out["Impact (1-10)"], errors="coerce")
    out["Risk Score (LxI)"] = out["Likelihood (1-10)"] * out["Impact (1-10)"]
    # Keep only requested columns
    for c in KEEP_COLS:
        if c not in out.columns:
            out[c] = ""
    return out[KEEP_COLS]
